[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA Jazzer fuzzing session flagged a critical security issue—file path traversal—in [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe Apache Commons Compress `Expander` example. The fuzzer’s input caused the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`FilePathTraversal` sanitizer to trip when the `Expander.expand` routine attempted [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto write files outside of the intended output directory. The stack trace identifies[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe sanitizer hook in `FilePathTraversal` and the call chain through multiple [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moverloads of `Expander.expand`, ultimately invoked by the `ExpanderFuzzer` harness.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- What the issue is  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  During fuzz testing of the Apache Commons Compress “Expander” example, a file [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpath traversal was detected. When expanding archive entries, the code resolved a [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpath that escaped the designated output directory [0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[35m/tmp/[0m[95mexpander-tmp[0m[39m…[0m[35m/output/q/r/[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, triggering the [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical` exception from Jazzer’s `FilePathTraversal` [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msanitizer.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability type  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  This is a file path traversal vulnerability: unvalidated or improperly sanitized [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfile paths allow creation or modification of files outside the intended directory.[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Important observations and findings  [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. The exception originates in [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`com.code_intelligence.jazzer.sanitizers.FilePathTraversal.check` and its hook [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmethod `pathFirstArgHook`.  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. The traversal is detected before any file write occurs, indicating the [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msanitizer is correctly intercepting unsafe paths.  [0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. The stack trace shows repeated calls to `Expander.expand` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mat lines [0m[1;36m86[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m204[0m[39m, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m324[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m400[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m460[0m[39m in `Expander.java`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, suggesting multiple overloads or recursive [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexpansion logic potentially mishandle entry names.  [0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. The harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`ExpanderFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput` at line [0m[1;36m52[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m supplies [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39marbitrary archive data to the `Expander`, but is not the root cause—merely the [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentry point for the fuzzer.[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Code areas to investigate  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. `org.apache.commons.compress.archivers.examples.Expander`  [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - All `expand` method overloads, especially how entry names are joined to the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moutput directory.  [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - Any canonicalization or sanitization of entry names prior to file system [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moperations.  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Archive entry processing  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - Logic that reads entry names, handles “..[0m[35m/[0m[39m” sequences, and resolves final [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpaths.  [0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Interaction with `FilePathTraversal`  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - Understand how the sanitizer hook is applied to the first argument of [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfile-writing methods and verify that the code under test invokes file I/O APIs in a[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mway that allows detection.  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Fuzzer harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`ExpanderFuzzer`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                            [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Canonicalize and resolve the output‐directory upfront in Expander.expand  [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. In every overload of `Expander.expand` that accepts a `File targetDirectory` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mor `Path targetDirectory`, replace the simple `[0m[1;35mtoPath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[35m/[0m[39m `[0m[1;35mnormalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` call with [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfull absolute, normalized, real‐path resolution.  [0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Change[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```java[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        final Path targetDirPath = targetDirectory == null ? null : [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mtargetDirectory.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        to[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```java[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        final Path raw = [0m[1;35mtargetDirectory.toPath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.toAbsolutePath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;35mFiles.createDirectories[0m[1;39m([0m[39mraw[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        final Path targetDirPath = [0m[1;35mraw.toRealPath[0m[1;39m([0m[39mLinkOption.NOFOLLOW_LINKS[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Import `java.nio.file.LinkOption`.  [0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. This ensures that the base directory is absolute, all symlinks in the base [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpath are resolved, and any “..[0m[35m/[0m[39m” pieces in the user‐supplied directory are [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39meliminated before any entry is written.[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Preserve and re­use existing resolveIn checks  [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Keep the current `ArchiveEntry.resolveIn` and `ZipArchiveEntry.resolveIn` [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlogic unmodified—both compute  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```java[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      Path outputFile = [0m[1;35mparentPath.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39mname[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35moutputFile.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Zip slip…"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Because `parentPath` is now guaranteed to be a canonical absolute directory, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthis check is sound: if an archive entry’s name attempts to climb out [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`..[0m[35m/[0m[95mfoo[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe normalized `outputFile` will no longer start with the canonical base, and an [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexception will be thrown.[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Update the `[0m[1;35mtoPath[0m[1;39m([0m[39mFile[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` helper  [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Modify[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```java[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      private Path [0m[1;35mtoPath[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfinal File targetDirectory[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          return targetDirectory != null ? [0m[1;35mtargetDirectory.toPath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m : null;[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      to[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```java[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      private Path [0m[1;35mtoPath[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfinal File targetDirectory[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m throws IOException [0m[1;39m{[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetDirectory == null[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              return null;[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          Path raw = [0m[1;35mtargetDirectory.toPath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.toAbsolutePath[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;35mFiles.createDirectories[0m[1;39m([0m[39mraw[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          return [0m[1;35mraw.toRealPath[0m[1;39m([0m[39mLinkOption.NOFOLLOW_LINKS[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Propagate `IOException` as needed into the public `expand` entry points.[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification and preservation of existing behavior  [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By resolving the base directory to an absolute, symlink‐free path before any [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfile creation, we guarantee the `startsWith` guard in `resolveIn` cannot be [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbypassed via symlinks or relative paths.  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We are not removing functionality or changing the archive‐entry processing [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpipeline; we only harden the base‐directory handling.  [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No harness, fuzzing‐logic, or external dependencies are modified—only core [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mapplication code. All existing `expand` overloads still funnel through the same [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlogic, so backwards compatibility and existing tests are preserved.[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Potential side effects and mitigation  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If the user supplies a non‐existent directory, we now always call [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mFiles.createDirectories[0m[1;39m([0m[39mraw[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` first, so the directory will be created [0m[1;39m([0m[39msame as [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbefore when the first entry is a directory[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Calling `toRealPath` throws if the directory does not exist; but since we [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcreate it immediately beforehand, this error path is safe.  [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If the directory is on a filesystem that does not support symlink resolution, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`toRealPath` may throw; in that rare case, we can catch and wrap with an [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Unable to resolve target directory: "[0m[39m + raw, e[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` to preserve existing[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexception semantics.[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. References in code  [0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `Expander.java: line [0m[1;36m68[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m71[0m[39m` for base‐dir canonicalization.  [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `Expander.java: line [0m[1;36m478[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m482[0m[39m` for the updated `toPath` helper.  [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No changes in `resolveIn` implementations [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m75[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m82[0m[39m in `ArchiveEntry.java` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand [0m[1;36m1484[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m1492[0m[39m in `ZipArchiveEntry.java`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, since they rely on the caller to supply a[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcorrect base path.[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mWith these changes, any attempt by an archive entry to traverse outside the [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mintended output directory will be caught early—either by the `startsWith` check or [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mby an `IOException` during base‐dir canonicalization—effectively eliminating the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfile‐path traversal vulnerability reported by Jazzer.[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
